# Sla Compiler Implementation Tasks

This document tracks the tasks and implementation progress of the Sla compiler plugin (`sa_plugin_sla`).

---

## Task List

### 0. Roadmap To 100% Y-Shared Direct SAB Completion
- [ ] **Operating Rules Until Completion**
  - [x] Active implementation workspace is `/home/vscode/projects/sa_plugins/sa_plugin_sla`. Do not switch implementation or task planning into `/home/vscode/projects/sla_ecs`; use `sla_ecs` only as an explicit host regression target such as `lib/parallel.sla`.
  - [x] Keep the architecture Y-shaped: `SLA source -> AST/typecheck -> shared frontend/shared lowering rules/std metadata -> {SA text emitter -> .sa -> sa compile, SAB structured emitter -> .sab -> sa compile}`.
  - [x] The shared layer is before the SA/SAB fork; direct SAB must stay direct and must not implement `.sla -> .sa text -> .sab` as the normal path.
  - [x] New semantics belong in `src/lowering_rules.zig`, shared frontend/typecheck results, `sla_std/std_surface.sla_meta`, or the `sa_std` macro/import surface. `src/sab_codegen.zig` should consume those contracts and emit SAB.
  - [x] Use `sa plugin install --dev .` as the official install/host verification gate; do not manually copy plugin artifacts.
  - [x] Report feature completion percentage, broader Y/shared-lowering percentage, direct SAB fallback-removal percentage, and current no-fallback sweep count after every completed feature.
  - [x] Commit only verified completed slices. Partial exploration stays uncommitted.
  - [x] If more than 10 verified feature slices accumulate without a commit, stop and recommend a batch commit; if the verified set is clean, commit the completed slices before continuing.
  - [x] Before each implementation slice, update this file with the target, owner phase, expected verification, architectural boundary, and progress estimate.
- [ ] **Progress Accounting Rules**
  - [ ] A feature slice is 100% only after local build, focused local no-fallback run, official `sa plugin install --dev .`, `SA_PLUGIN_DEV=1 sa sla help`, focused host no-fallback run, SA-text parity when applicable, relevant regressions, docs/progress updates, and `git diff --check`.
  - [ ] If a slice fixes only the direct SAB tail but leaves duplicated lowering decisions outside `lowering_rules.zig`, shared frontend, or `sla_std/std_surface.sla_meta`, count it as a partial bug fix and keep the Y/shared task open.
  - [ ] Do not treat fallback success as direct-SAB progress unless the fallback use is removed or documented as an explicitly unsupported surface with a concrete future task.
  - [ ] Use this percent scale: 0% not started, 25% design/owner identified, 50% implementation drafted and builds, 75% focused local no-fallback filters pass, 90% full local fixture/regressions pass, 100% host install/help/host regressions/sweep/docs/diff-check complete.
  - [ ] Keep global numbers conservative: a draft that has not passed host `sa plugin install --dev .` and `SA_PLUGIN_DEV=1 sa sla help` does not move global Y/shared-lowering or fallback-removal percentages.
- [ ] **P1 Short-Term Stability, Labels, And Benchmark Formalization**
  - [ ] Push `sa_plugin_sla` direct-SAB no-fallback from the historical 58/69 baseline to 69/69 as a key mainline stability metric for moving Sla from usable-with-fallback to truly stable direct SAB. Current newer tracked corpus is above that historical denominator, but this P1 task remains the canonical short-term metric until the old 69-file set is explicitly mapped and closed.
  - [x] Provide compiler-side stability metadata support for downstream projects: a manifest/schema and verification output that can record labels such as `stable-demo`, `verified-sa-backend`, `verified-sab-backend`, `experimental-parallel`, and `shape-only-reflect`. This repo must not define or maintain `sla_ecs` labels directly; it only supplies the contract/tooling that downstream projects can consume. Implemented by `src/stability_metadata.zig`, `sa sla stability schema`, `sa sla stability verify <manifest.json> [--json]`, `sap.json` help, and `docs/stability_metadata_cn.md`; verified with focused Zig tests, full `zig build`, full `zig build test` (90/90), local/installed CLI smoke, `sa plugin install --dev .`, and `SA_PLUGIN_DEV=1 sa sla help`.
  - [x] Add standalone benchmark harness coverage and publish it as a formal benchmark track owned by this repo: `.sla -> .sab` cold/warm compile time, `.sla -> native` build time, and SAB fallback vs direct SAB. Domain throughput such as ECS spawn/query/schedule is exposed through configurable external benchmark commands/hooks, not implemented as `sla_ecs` business logic in this compiler repo. Implemented by `tools/bench_sla_pipeline.sh` plus `docs/benchmarking_cn.md`; smoke verified with `bash -n`, `--runs 1 --skip-native`, full built-in `--runs 1`, and `--external 'noop::true'` JSONL output.
- [ ] **P2 Medium-Term Generation, Formal, And Version Semantics**
  - [ ] Provide the compiler-side generated-source support needed by downstream composition-runner generators: stable schema inputs, import/codegen contracts, typecheck hooks, and verification metadata. Do not maintain `sla_ecs` runner generation in this repo; downstream projects own their generated runner specs and outputs.
  - [ ] Turn the `sci` Referee formal verification roadmap into an executable plan. The README-level Coq/Lean4 high-assurance direction needs a staged implementation route if high assurance is a core project claim.
  - [ ] Establish explicit version semantics across the three repos: semver policy, changelog discipline, and a compatibility matrix. Account for `sci` currently declaring `0.0.1` in `build.zig.zon` while build scripts can derive versions from git tags.
- [ ] **Current Recovery Point For Next Context**
	- [x] Added non-identifier/call-expression postfix try sources inside user macros (2026-07-12). Shared `macroBodyHasTry()` detects whether expansion can early-return, while TypeChecker separately resolves propagated container parameters through nested macro calls. An ordinary call expression `direct_macro_make_option(value, succeed)?` therefore creates call-site cleanup without excluding value/succeed. Some(36) reaches Some(42); None early-returns and releases Box, result, and scalar params in both emitters. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, Option SA/SAB 1/1, filtered custom try SAB 3/3, owner SA/SAB 15/15, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for tracked identifier/nested/call-expression Option/Result/custom Result macro try; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next choose match guards or Option/Result macro matches.
	- [x] Added direct-SAB scalar comparison guards for user-defined enum matches, including user-macro expansion (2026-07-12). Shared `supportsScalarMatchGuard()` classifies identifier-vs-identifier/integer comparisons. Guarded-case scalar payload bindings and guard result registers are preallocated before the ladder, so tag mismatch and guard failure have identical capability state; remaining case-condition registers are released only after guard success. The fixture covers true guard -> 42 and false guard -> repeated-variant fallback -> 8. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, enum SA/SAB 2/2, borrowed enum SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for the focused scalar guard surface; complex/call guards and Option/Result direct-SAB matches remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added Option/Result pattern matching inside user macros for direct SAB (2026-07-12). TypeChecker infers `Option<infer>` / `Result<infer,infer>` from standard macro patterns. At concrete expansion, direct SAB resolves the match value through the caller-local concrete type and uses the macro assignment target type for the result slot. `genMatch` consumes shared `planLetPattern()` and the existing Option/Result std fragments for checks and payload extraction. Some(41) and Ok(40) return 42; None returns 0; Err(7) returns -7 in SA/SAB. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, Option SA/SAB 1/1, Result SA/SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for unguarded Option/Result macro match; complex guards and standard-match guards remain separate; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Extended direct-SAB scalar match guards to Option/Result payloads inside user macros (2026-07-12). Guarded standard payload bindings use the same preallocated capability-stable registers as guarded user-enum bindings, while checks and extraction remain shared through `planLetPattern()` and Option/Result std fragments. Some(41) with floor 40 and Ok(40) with floor 39 return 42; low Some(9) and Ok(8) fail the guard and reach repeated-variant fallbacks returning -9/-8; None and Err remain correct. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SA/SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for scalar standard-container guards; call/compound guards remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added compound scalar match guards joined by `&&`/`||` for direct SAB and user macros (2026-07-12). Shared `scalarMatchGuardTempCount()` recursively validates comparison leaves and owns exact scratch-count planning. Direct SAB preallocates all guard scratch registers before the ladder and emits the tree postorder, preserving identical capability states on tag mismatch, guard failure, and success. `inner > floor && inner < ceiling` returns 42 in range and sends low/high Some values to the repeated fallback (-9/-21). Verified with focused shared-plan test, build 7/7, full Zig 209/209, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for recursive comparison/logical guard trees; call-expression guards remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added ordinary static call-expression match guards with identifier arguments for direct SAB and user macros (2026-07-12). Shared guard planning assigns one scratch to an eligible call. Static-call emission accepts a preallocated destination, preventing a guard-only result register from appearing on just the matched path; restricting args to identifiers avoids conditional materialization temporaries. `direct_macro_guard_between(inner, floor, ceiling)` guards Result Ok: 40 returns 42, low/high Ok values fall through to -8/-21, and Err returns -7 in SA/SAB. Verified with shared-plan coverage, build 7/7, full Zig 209/209, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for identifier-argument static call guards; materialized call args remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added integer-literal arguments to ordinary static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared guard planning accepts identifier/integer-literal args. Direct SAB writes literals directly into the call operand text, so no guard-only argument registers are created, and continues writing the call result into preallocated scratch. `direct_macro_guard_between(inner, 39, 41)` returns true for Ok(40), while Ok(8)/Ok(21) reach repeated fallbacks and Err remains correct in SA/SAB. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 209/209, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for identifier/integer-literal static call guards; general expression/materialized args remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added recursively materialized integer-arithmetic arguments to static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared planning counts `+`/`-`/`*`/`/`/`%` argument nodes plus the call result, and direct SAB emits each arithmetic node into the preallocated guard scratch set. `direct_macro_guard_between(inner + 1, 40, 42)` succeeds for Ok(40); low/high Ok values reach -8/-21 fallbacks and Err remains -7 in SA/SAB. Focused shared-plan coverage proves one arithmetic node plus call result uses two scratches. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 209/209, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for integer arithmetic call args; other materialized argument shapes remain open; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep.
	- [x] Added primitive cast arguments around supported scalar expressions in static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared planning counts the cast node; direct SAB materializes focused `i64/u64` integer casts into preallocated scratch. `direct_macro_guard_between((inner + 1) as i64, 40, 42)` succeeds for Ok(40), low/high Ok values reach -8/-21 fallbacks, and Err remains -7 in SA/SAB. Focused shared-plan coverage proves arithmetic + cast + call uses three scratches. 	- [x] Added scalar field-projection arguments to static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared planning accepts `identifier.field` and counts its load scratch. Direct SAB caches macro value parameters with their concrete call-site types, so ordinary match lowering can resolve shared struct field layouts during expansion. The Result guard uses `limits.floor`/`limits.ceiling` from `DirectMacroGuardLimits`; Ok success, low/high fallback, and Err paths pass SA/SAB. Focused shared-plan coverage confirms field scratch counting. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 209/209, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, rosetta 30 SAB 1/1, Option SAB 1/1, Result SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. 	- [x] Added fixed-array constant-index arguments to static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared planning accepts `identifier[nonnegative integer literal]` and counts its load scratch. Direct SAB consumes the cached macro parameter's concrete array type and shared `arrayElementLayout()` to load into preallocated scratch. The Result guard uses `limits[0]`/`limits[1]` from `[i64; 2]`; Ok success, low/high fallback, and Err paths pass SA/SAB. Focused shared-plan coverage confirms index scratch counting. 	- [x] Added fixed-array dynamic identifier index arguments to static call match guards (2026-07-12). Shared planning reserves offset, element-pointer, and loaded-value scratches. Direct SAB consumes shared array stride/layout facts and emits multiply + pointer-add + load into the preallocated set. The Result guard uses `limits[floor_index]`/`limits[ceiling_index]`; Ok success, low/high fallback, and Err paths pass SA/SAB. 	- [x] Extended macro postfix `?` through nested user macros and standard/custom Result (2026-07-12). TypeChecker recursively follows parameters forwarded into another macro's try source, keyed by macro/parameter with a visiting set, and direct `?param` is an always-consume ownership effect. The outer concrete call now records the caller cleanup used by the inner try. Standard Result Ok(34) becomes Ok(42), Err(7) propagates; custom Result success becomes 42 and error 6 propagates, all through a wrapper and with Box/result cleanup on error. Option coverage remains green. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, filtered custom try SA/SAB 3/3, Result SA/SAB 1/1, owner SA/SAB 15/15, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for tracked direct-identifier Option/Result/custom Result macro try plus nested forwarding; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next select match guards, Option/Result macro match inference, or non-identifier try sources as a distinct surface.
	- [x] Added Option postfix `?` inside user macros with call-site early-return cleanup (2026-07-12). Shared rules identify macro parameters used as try sources. TypeChecker accepts infer macro try bodies and stores cleanup names against each concrete `CallExpr`, excluding the propagated container argument so the early return transfers it. SA and SAB carry the invocation list during expansion; SA resolves macro-context inner types, while SAB feeds the same type into ordinary `genTry()` and uses its existing branch/result lifecycle. A move-parameter function with Box cleanup returns Some(42) for Some(33), and returns None while cleaning Box/result locals for None. Verified with shared rule assertion, build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, filtered/custom try SA/SAB 3/3, owner SA/SAB 15/15, borrow-temp SAB 25/25, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for Option macro try; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next cover Result/custom Result and nested macro try forwarding with the same per-call metadata.
	- [x] Closed same-name SA inline hygiene inside value-producing user-macro unsafe blocks (2026-07-12). Codegen records the active inline macro, applies hygienic aliases and macro-local type overrides to unsafe block prefix lets, keeps them active for tail evaluation, and resolves attached cleanup through the alias. Caller and unsafe-local are both named `local`; SA previously consumed the caller and failed at `result + local`, while both backends now return 135. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, Box unsafe SA/SAB 1/1, owner SA/SAB 15/15, borrow-temp SAB 25/25, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Postfix try is the next distinct macro gap and requires shared call-site early-return cleanup metadata.
	- [x] Added value-producing `unsafe` blocks inside user macros for direct SAB (2026-07-12). The macro-specific unsafe path resolves contextual result type, scopes hygienic macro locals, stores the tail through the existing result-slot transfer helper, releases block locals, and reloads transferred state. The fixture uses an explicitly typed unsafe-local and a separate caller local, returning 135 in SA/SAB. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, Box unsafe SA/SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, borrow-temp SAB 25/25, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100% for the focused unsafe surface; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Postfix try remains open pending shared macro call-site early-return cleanup; exact same-name SA caller/unsafe-local shadowing remains a recursive inline-hygiene follow-up.
	- [x] Added user-defined enum `match` inside user macros (2026-07-12). Shared TypeChecker match inference now uses the first enum-qualified pattern to concretize an infer-typed macro scrutinee, updates the macro parameter symbol and `expr_types`, and checks all arms against the same enum. Value-only macro parameter caching then lets both emitters reuse ordinary match lowering rather than duplicating branch/result-slot policy in macro codegen. The payload macro match returns 36 in SA/SAB. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, ordinary enum SA/SAB 2/2, borrowed enum SA/SAB 1/1, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next select postfix try or unsafe macro lowering; Option/Result match and guards remain separate if they need new lifecycle rules.
	- [x] Completed common expression-container traversal for user-macro ownership effects (2026-07-12). Shared scanning now composes binary, field, index, slice, cast, borrow, deref, try, and await children. The runtime macro `out = *^value` returns 37 in SA/SAB. SA deref lowering now removes the capability prefix before using the source as a load address; the previous `load ^source+0` produced `UnknownRegister`. `tests/diagnostics/user_macro_deref_move_use_after.sla` confirms caller reuse is `UseAfterMove`. Verified with shared rule coverage, build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, three macro diagnostics, Box raw SA/SAB 1/1, owner SAB 15/15, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Explicit-move expression traversal is closed; next select a distinct macro lowering surface such as match/try/unsafe.
	- [x] Extended user-macro ownership-effect traversal through aggregate literal containers (2026-07-12). Shared `macroNodeConsumption()` now composes struct field/update, enum payload, tuple, array, and repeat-array child effects. The positive macro moves a Box into `DirectMacroBoxHolder.value` and returns 38 in SA/SAB; `tests/diagnostics/user_macro_aggregate_move_use_after.sla` reuses the caller source and receives installed `UseAfterMove`, proving TypeChecker owns the effect rather than depending on emitter-local state. Verified with shared rule coverage, build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, conditional and aggregate diagnostics, smart-pointer SA/SAB 3/3, owner SAB 15/15, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next complete expression-container traversal for binary/index/cast/borrow/deref/try/await shapes.
	- [x] Propagated user-macro ownership consumption through ordinary function move-parameter calls (2026-07-12). Shared macro-effect analysis now descends into call arguments, and shared `rootIdentifier()` unwraps move/borrow expressions so `macroParamRequiresLvalue()` sees `^value` passed to a typed move parameter. SA-text prefixed call arguments resolve through the active macro alias rather than emitting the literal macro parameter name. The focused Box macro calls `direct_macro_consume_box(^value)` and returns 39; previously SAB passed but SA emitted invalid `^value`, and frontend cleanup lacked the caller effect. Verified with shared rule test, build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, conditional diagnostic, fn-ptr SA/SAB 12/12, owner SA/SAB 15/15, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next extend explicit-move effect traversal through aggregate and other expression containers.
	- [x] Added path-sensitive user-macro parameter consumption effects (2026-07-12). Shared `control_flow_rules.MacroParamConsumption` and sequence/branch composition distinguish never, always, and conditional consumption. Two consuming `if` arms are always; one consuming arm is conditional; for/while body consumption is conditional because zero iterations remain possible. TypeChecker carries the three-state result through nested user-macro calls and emits `MacroConditionalConsume` rather than marking the caller unconditionally consumed. Positive macro coverage moves a Box on both true/false branches; `tests/diagnostics/user_macro_conditional_move.sla` forwards through a wrapper to a one-branch inner move and matches the installed error. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 208/208, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, installed diagnostic, owner SA/SAB 15/15, smart-pointer SAB 3/3, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next extend effect classification through ordinary functions with move parameters invoked from macro bodies.
	- [x] Propagated ownership consumption through nested user-macro calls (2026-07-12). TypeChecker now recursively resolves whether a macro parameter is forwarded to a consuming parameter of another user macro. Direct effects continue to come from shared `control_flow_rules.macroParamConsumesValue()`; the frontend adds call-graph resolution keyed by `(macro declaration, parameter index)` and a visiting set prevents recursion cycles from looping. The wrapper-to-inner Box move previously passed SAB only because nested emitter expansion marked the register, while SA later emitted stale source cleanup; both backends now return 40. Verified with build 7/7, full Zig 207/207, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, owner SA/SAB 15/15, smart-pointer SA/SAB 3/3, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next resolve conditional macro consumption path semantics instead of treating any consuming branch as an unconditional move.
	- [x] Closed user-macro explicit move ownership propagation across frontend, SA-text, and direct SAB (2026-07-12). `control_flow_rules.macroParamConsumesValue()` provides a pure recursive body classifier for direct move/release effects; TypeChecker consumes the corresponding caller identifier at the macro call. Direct SAB's macro move path marks the substituted register consumed. SA assignment/storage lowering uses the underlying register rather than the call-argument-only `^reg` spelling and transfers lifecycle state from that register. The Box regression originally failed SAB with source cleanup UseAfterMove and SA with invalid `destination = ^source`; both now return 42. Verified with shared rule test, build 7/7, full Zig 207/207, local/installed macro SA/SAB 2/2, owner SA/SAB 15/15, Box raw 1/1, smart-pointer 3/3, shallow-copy 3/3, imported-macro SAB 11/11, official install/help, and host `parallel.sla` SA/SAB 1/1. Feature 100%; Y/shared-lowering remains about 99%; fallback-removal remains 100%; authoritative corpus remains 130/130 without a new sweep. Next extend consumption effects through nested user-macro calls rather than duplicating emitter-local guesses.
	- [x] Added direct-SAB user-macro enum literal construction (2026-07-12). Macro expression lowering now consumes the shared enum discriminant index, ABI size, tag offset, variant lookup, payload lookup, and field layout contracts while evaluating each payload value through the active macro substitution context. The regression covers `DirectMacroMessage::Pair { left, right }` from macro parameters and the unit `DirectMacroMessage::Empty`, assigns each through a caller lvalue, and matches afterward to prove tag/payload and replacement semantics. After constants were deduplicated and hoisted, the decisive remaining bug was in `cloneDecodedModuleFunctionSig()`: it rebuilt cloned helper `reg_ids` only from params plus renamed locals, so stable constant ids skipped by local remapping never entered `sa_set_insert`'s function scope. `src/sab_codegen.zig` now deduplicates/hoists filtered constants, records stable const ids, and remaps the verified source signature's complete `reg_ids` before adding cloned-local extras. 	- [x] Fixed plain and generic for-in protocol pruning (2026-07-11). SLA for-in over a user type depends implicitly on `iter_len` and `iter_at`; those calls are not explicit `call_expr` nodes. Pre-typecheck syntactic reachability therefore removed the impl and produced `Iterable` mismatch. After retaining the impl there, post-typecheck emit reachability still removed both methods, so direct SAB emitted protocol calls without declarations and failed `UnknownRegister` callee. `src/plugin_reachability.zig` now marks typed `iter_len`/`iter_at` associated candidates for protocol for-in, with the existing conservative fallback for an inferred generic local whose type is not yet syntactically known. `src/plugin_emit_reachability.zig` uses checked expression types and `TypeChecker.methodForType()` to retain the exact methods in final output. Extended `sla pre-typecheck pruning keeps for-in protocol methods` to verify pre-typecheck method retention, TypeChecker, and post-typecheck reachability. Focused verification only: Zig regression, `zig build`, official dev install, `test_unit_for_in_protocol.sla` and `test_unit_generic_for_in_protocol.sla` SA 2/2 plus strict SAB 2/2. No full suite/corpus rerun. Last full audit remains 120/130; focused closures leave 4 known files.
	- [x] Fixed pre-typecheck pruning of local function-pointer callee bindings (2026-07-11). The project-snapshot shortcut pass applies a dead-pure-let cleanup to all test bodies. Identifier and field initializers are considered pure, but shared identifier-usage analysis previously ignored `call.func_name`, so `let f = fn_ptr_inc; f(4)` and `let f = holder.f; f(1)` lost `f` before TypeChecker and failed as `Undefined call: f`; the Vec-index form survived only because index expressions are not in the pure-expression set. `src/plugin_reachability.zig` now treats a plain non-associated callee name as an identifier use. 	- [x] Fixed direct-SAB stack-allocation cleanup `StackEscape` regressions (2026-07-11). `test_unit_array_to_slice_call.sla`, `test_unit_async_while_let_future_queue_direct.sla`, and `test_unit_derive_semantics.sla` all ended temporary stack slots through generic `emitRelease`; non-owning stack regs were translated to `move_`, which the SAB verifier correctly rejected as moving stack storage out of the function. `src/sab_codegen.zig` now treats a register recorded by `emitStackAlloc` as function-stack lifetime: cleanup updates compiler release/readiness metadata without emitting `move_` or `release`. Array-to-slice call materialization also leaves the temporary Slice slot stack-managed while still releasing a temporary backing array when required. 	- [x] Fixed direct-SAB sibling-scope plain `let` register aliasing (2026-07-11). The prior `str_end` fix only deduplicated repeated `stack_alloc` for mutable scalar bindings; ordinary same-named bindings still interned to one function-global register id. In `sla_tsgo` `scan_ident`, the early-return `let id_len` consumed/released that id and the post-loop `let id_len` reused it, producing `UseAfterMove`/`UnknownRegister`. `src/sab_codegen.zig` now scans each function/test body for names declared by `let` more than once and gives each occurrence a fresh register while preserving source-name lookup through the lexical `locals` stack. 		- [x] Fixed pre-existing materialize-fixpoint OOM (use-after-free) surfaced by the full test run (2026-07-10). ROOT CAUSE: `materializeReachableImportedModuleBodies` (in `src/plugin_reachability.zig`) reparses imported modules in a fixpoint until `stringSetsEqual(selected_functions, module.parsed_function_bodies)`. `reparseModuleWithSelectedBodies` (in `src/plugin_module_table.zig`) was storing the *borrowed* selected key pointers into `module.parsed_function_bodies`, then calling `module.exports.deinit()` which frees the mangled method-symbol key strings (e.g. `ImportedThing_inherent`) that those pointers alias; the next `buildFromDecls` reused that arena space, so `parsed_function_bodies` held dangling/garbage keys. The content-hashed comparison therefore never matched, the fixpoint never converged, and each iteration reparsed the module into the shared arena unbounded -> ~3.6 GiB -> OOM-kill on low-RAM hosts. (Reachable set was already stable at 7 entries by iteration 2, confirmed via temporary iteration/set-diff instrumentation; the loop ran to a 200-iteration guard.) FIX: `reparseModuleWithSelectedBodies` now `self.allocator.dupe`s each selected name into owned copies BEFORE `module.exports.deinit()`, so the tracking keys stay valid and stable; the fixpoint converges in ~3 iterations. Confirmed pre-existing (committed `HEAD` OOMs identically at 3.58 GiB via git-worktree A/B), so the refactor did not cause it. Verification: focused test 3.6 GiB->6.4 MB pass; all four previously-OOM batches pass; whole 166-test batched suite 165/166; `zig fmt --check` + `zig build --summary all` 7/7.
		- [x] Fixed pre-existing lazy-transitive bare-cross-module-call discovery bug (2026-07-10). ROOT CAUSE: on the lazy-transitive import path (small roots: <=64 decls and <=32KB, `prune_for_test_codegen`), `discoverContributingChildSlaModules` (in `src/plugin_import_expand.zig`) only pulled in a transitively-imported `.sla` module when the reachable/referenced sets contained a namespace-qualified `ns__name` key (via `resolvedSlaImportNamespaceIsReferenced`). A BARE (unqualified) cross-module call — e.g. `wrapper.sla` calling `program_new_single_file` defined in transitively-imported `compiler.sla` — lands in the sets as the plain exported name (no `ns__` prefix), and an unresolved bare call goes into `referenced_types` (not `reachable`), so the defining module was never discovered -> `Undefined call: program_new_single_file`. This intermittently presented (stale-binary races) but is deterministic. FIX: added `moduleExportsReferencedBareSymbol`, which defensively parses a namespace-unreferenced child (`getOrParse catch continue` — a genuinely dead/invalid child is still skipped, preserving the `skips unreferenced child imports` / dead-grandchild regressions) and pulls it in only if it exports a function/method name present in `reachable` OR `referenced_types`, or a const/macro/type name in `referenced_types`. Confirmed pre-existing (fails identically on committed `HEAD`). Verification: test 131 fail->pass, run 5x deterministic; dead/unreferenced-child + lazy-transitive regressions (idx 105-113) all pass; whole 166-test batched suite **166/166 twice**; `zig fmt --check` + `zig build --summary all` 7/7.
		- [x] Fixed direct-SAB `RegisterRedefinition` on sibling-scope stack-slot `let` (2026-07-10, commit `1521d7c`). ROOT CAUSE: register identity in `src/sab_codegen.zig` is name-keyed and function-global (`intern(name)` returns one id per name for the whole function). Two sibling-scope `let` bindings of the same name — e.g. `let mut str_end` in two separate `if` blocks (as in `sla_tsgo` `members/emitter/src/emitter.sla`, string-literal scan for `"` and `'`) — resolve to a single register id. A `mut` scalar binding uses a stack slot (`bindingNeedsScalarReassignSlot`), and stack-slot locals are never killed by scope-exit release, so `emitStackAlloc` emitted `stack_alloc <id>` twice for the same id on a straight-line path (THEN_0 -> MERGE -> THEN_5), tripping the SAB verifier's `RegisterRedefinition`. FIX: added `stack_alloc_emitted` set (cleared per-function in `beginFunction`); `emitStackAlloc` allocates the slot once per register id and treats a repeat as a no-op (the two bindings never coexist and share type/size, so the caller's store overwrites the reused slot). Minimal repro `tests/test_unit_sibling_scope_stack_slot_let_direct.sla`. Confirmed pre-existing (independent of the plugin split). Verification: repro fail->pass; whole 166-test batched suite **166/166 twice**; downstream `sla_ecs` direct-SAB smokes pass (~1.5 GiB peak); `zig fmt --check` + `zig build --summary all` 7/7. NOTE: this un-blocks one layer of `docs/sab_compile_emit_text_timeout_issue_cn.md`; the next surface on `sla_tsgo` `tests/test_program_emit_text_contract.sla` is a `UseAfterMove` on register `ti` (trap 1009), still open.

- [ ] **Final 100% Acceptance Checklist**
  - [ ] Local compiler health: `zig fmt`, `zig build --summary all`, `zig build test --summary all`, and `git diff --check` all pass.
  - [ ] Official plugin health: `sa plugin install --dev .` completes from this repo, and `SA_PLUGIN_DEV=1 sa sla help` shows the SLA CLI surface from the installed dev plugin.

This item must be re-run if implementation or fixture files change before final completion.

  - [ ] Macro-expansion health: macro fixtures pass no-fallback without SAB-only macro semantics, and any macro-shaped failure is either fixed or reclassified to a concrete shared call/std/import task.
  - [ ] Borrow/precedence health: focused borrow, smart-pointer, RefCell, address-of-field/index/deref, branch, loop, call-argument, and early-return fixtures pass direct SAB no-fallback and SA-text parity where applicable.
  - [ ] Y-shared health: every remaining high-level semantic decision has a shared owner; no new feature is implemented only as a type/library-name branch in `src/sab_codegen.zig`.
  - [ ] Fallback health: normal SAB path has no unowned fallback use in the tracked unit corpus; any unsupported surface is named by fixture, lowering kind, owner phase, and future contract.
  - [ ] Documentation health: `progress.md` records final feature percent, Y/shared-lowering percent, direct SAB fallback-removal percent, and full sweep counts; `tasks.md` has no stale current-blocker notes.
  - [ ] Commit health: all verified completed slices are committed, and the final commit message names the shared rule/metadata contracts plus the exact verification gates.
- [ ] **Commit And Documentation Rules For 100% Completion**
  - [ ] Never commit a slice that only moves the failing symptom; commit only after the slice's local and host gates pass and `progress.md` records feature percent, Y/shared-lowering percent, direct SAB fallback-removal percent, and full no-fallback sweep count.

### 1. Lexer & Parser Updates
- [x] **Postfix `?` Operator Support**
  - [x] Add `?` token tag to `src/lexer.zig`.
  - [x] Update `lexer.zig` scanner to scan postfix `?` token.
  - [x] Update `src/parser.zig` to parse postfix `?` operator.
- [x] **Generic Struct Literal Support**
  - [x] Parse `Type<T> { field: value }` without adding any new keyword.
  - [x] Keep source cleanup implicit; no `drop` keyword or `drop()` function is introduced.

### 2. Type Checker & Symbol Resolver (Semantic Analyzer)
- [x] **Scope Builder & Symbol Table**
  - [x] Implement nested block scope stack.
  - [x] Track local variable declarations, parameter bindings, and constant values.
- [x] **Type Resolver**
  - [x] Parse and resolve primitive types (`int`, `float`, `bool`, `void`, `ptr`).
  - [x] Bind user-defined structs.
  - [x] Register signatures from FFI contract parser (`.sai`/`.sal`).
- [x] **Borrow Checker & Ownership Validator**
  - [x] Track variable ownership states (`Active` vs `Consumed`).
  - [x] Check move semantics (`^` transfer) and reject use-after-move.
  - [x] Validate borrow rules (`&` reference) and forbid mutable/immutable aliasing conflicts.

### 3. Monomorphization Engine
- [x] **Generic Collection & Instantiation**
  - [x] Traverse the AST to gather all generic struct instantiations and generic function calls.
  - [x] Map generic type parameters (like `T`) to concrete types (like `int`).
  - [x] Generate specialized non-generic structs and functions (e.g. `Option_int_Layout`, `unwrap_or_int`).

### 4. AST to SA Lowerer (Code Generation)
- [x] **Control Flow Flattener**
  - [x] Lower `if/else` conditional expressions into flat, conditional jumps with automated register cleanups before merge targets (preventing `PhiStateConflict`).
  - [x] Lower `switch` pattern matching expressions to flat conditional equality ladders.
- [x] **Hygienic Macro Expander**
  - [x] Perform compile-time Alpha-conversion (renaming local macro variables to globally unique names).
  - [x] Lower `macro` definitions and calls directly to SA's `[MACRO]` / `EXPAND` preprocessor statements.
- [x] **Scope Lifetime Auto-Cleanup Generator**
  - [x] Track active resources at block exits.
  - [x] Automatically inject SA `!reg` cleanup before scope endings so user `.sla` code does not need explicit releases.
- [x] **Loop Allocation Hoister**
  - [x] Detect `stack_alloc` statements inside `for` loops.
  - [x] Hoist allocations outside and before the loop label, reusing memory inside the loop body.
- [x] **Postfix `?` Unwrapper**
  - [x] Lower `expr?` into a conditional error check, injecting automated local variable cleanups and an early `return Err(^err)` on error branch.
- [x] **Struct Literal Lowering**
  - [x] Lower Sla struct literals to flat SA `alloc N` plus `store base+offset` instructions.
  - [x] Keep struct layouts as compile-time Sla metadata instead of emitting forbidden `#struct { ... }` brace syntax into `.sa`.

### 8. Sla Unit Test Framework (`@test`)
- [x] **Lexer: `@` token + comparison operators**
  - [x] `at` token tag for `@` symbol (no new keyword).
  - [x] `==`, `!=`, `<=`, `>=` two-char token tags added to lexer.
- [x] **AST: `TestDecl` node**
  - [x] `TestDecl` struct in `src/ast.zig`: `name`, `is_ignored`, `should_panic`, `body`.
  - [x] `test_decl: TestDecl` variant added to `Node` union.
- [x] **Parser: `@test` declaration parsing**
  - [x] Parses `@test [ignored] [should_panic] "name"() { ... }` syntax.
  - [x] No new keywords consumed — `ignored` and `should_panic` are identifiers.
  - [x] New comparison ops (`==`, `!=`, `<=`, `>=`) parsed in `parseInfixExpr`.
- [x] **Type Checker: `checkTest`**
  - [x] Type checks test body as void-returning, no-parameter block.
  - [x] `panic()` recognized as built-in void intrinsic.
  - [x] `if` condition accepts integer comparisons (0/1) in addition to booleans.
- [x] **Monomorphizer: `test_decl` traversal**
  - [x] Specializes generic calls inside test bodies.
- [x] **Codegen: `genTestDecl`**
  - [x] Emits `@test [ignored] [should_panic] "name"():` SA header.
  - [x] Unique entry labels per test (`L_TEST_ENTRY_N`).
  - [x] `panic(code)` lowered to SA `panic(code)` syntax.
  - [x] Loop allocation hoisting works inside test bodies.
- [x] **CLI: `sa sla test <file.sla> [options]`**
  - [x] Defaults to `--test-backend auto`, compiling `.sla` to managed SAB under `.sla-cache/sab/` and spawning `sa test <file.sab>`.
  - [x] Supports `--test-backend sab` for explicit SAB output and `--test-backend sa` for the legacy `.sla` -> `.test.sa` temp file path.
  - [x] Strips plugin-only `--test-backend` before forwarding remaining args to `sa test`.
  - [x] Applies `--filter` pruning before monomorphization/type checking on both SAB and SA test paths to keep focused tests small.
  - [x] Skill entry added: `sla test <file> [--test-backend auto|sab|sa] [sa-test-options...]`.
- [x] **Example test files**
  - [x] `tests/test_unit_basic.sla` — add/factorial/counter/ignored tests.
  - [x] `tests/test_unit_panic.sla` — `should_panic` and `ignored+should_panic`.
  - [x] `tests/test_unit_generics.sla` — `Option<T>` generics inside `@test`.
